FROM `Conversations` AS `c`
INNER JOIN `Bots` AS `b` ON `c`.`bot_id` = `b`.`id`
LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT `t`.`RawContent`, `t`.`Timestamp`, `t`.`Type`, 1 AS `c`
    FROM (
        SELECT `m`.`message_text` AS `RawContent`, `m`.`created_at` AS `Timestamp`, 'text' AS `Type`
        FROM `Messages` AS `m`
        WHERE `m`.`conversation_id` = `c`.`Id`
        UNION ALL
        SELECT `c0`.`file_name` AS `RawContent`, `c0`.`uploaded_at` AS `Timestamp`, CASE
            WHEN `c0`.`file_type` LIKE 'image%' THEN 'image'
            ELSE 'file'
        END AS `Type`
        FROM `chat_uploaded_files` AS `c0`
        WHERE `c0`.`conversation_id` = `c`.`Id`
    ) AS `t`
    ORDER BY `t`.`Timestamp` DESC
    LIMIT 1
